--- 帖子 #18 ---
Yes, that's true. In a trend this is great. But the best results is when you get a countertrend. The crossovers often show an indication of trendreversal. But in ranging markets it wil just keep bouncing around.

That's the only part of the system that is not mechanical. You have to 'feel' if it is going to bounce. If the crossovers are 'stronger' and 'sharper' then it is more likely that it is not going to bounce!

--- 帖子 #26 ---
I'm not sure you can backtest a system like this. When you look back over the charts, you'll see several crosses that appear to be entry and exit points. These crosses followed through to some degree and usually produce winning trades. What you won't see, however, is when a cross occurred, then quickly reversed. When you look back on this event, it will not show that the lines ever crossed at all. When backtesting, you will not record this as an entry because you will not see a cross.

I'm not saying that this isn't a good system with a lot of potential. I'm just wondering if there is a way to accurately backtest it.

Anyway, I appreciate all the info on this thread. If I'm wrong, please don't hesitate to tell me.

--- 帖子 #29 ---
Sidus,

I have taken just a cursory look at your method and it looks like these crossovers capture some momentum trades. But like all methods that use lagging indicators, you give up a lot at tops and bottoms.

May I suggest you look at the fib numbers from your entry point for taking profit. Depending on the volatility of the currency pair, you can move up or down from 21,34,55,89,144,233,and 377 pips. Just eyeballing your euro chart in the *.pdf, the fibs would have caught some good bottoms and tops. I wonder what optimum fib level is best for euro?

After you are out of a position, you simply wait for the next signal.

Keep learning.

Cheers.

--- 帖子 #38 ---
Ok, this is a moving average cross system.  They're as common as cockroaches and they all have the same problem, which is lag on the entry, which cuts down on your profits since you miss a lot of movement and chops you up in ranging or choppy markets.

Just letting you know beforehand.  I think most new traders start out with moving average crosses.  Wait till you go down the rabbit hole and start looking at fibonacci confluences, market profile and auction theory, etc.  The game gets a lot more interesting at that point.

--- 帖子 #75 ---
Hi hondakorn,

Perhaps it was just a typo on your part, but going long the Euro and short the Swissy at the same time is not hedging.  What you are doing is essentially doubling your position.  Doing this is virtually the same as doubling your position on either the Euro OR the Swissy.

Doing any of the above is okay as long as it fits within the risk parameters of your money management method.  But I don't see any point in doing it the way you are.

Did I misunderstand your intent here?

Dial

--- 帖子 #91 ---
I'm just trying to push you to the next level.  Don't take it as an attack. but I repeat, Sidus, why does your system work?  It's not sufficient to say "well, when this line crosses this line, price goes up or down accordingly."  What causes that relationship to exist?

It's kind of like somebody asking you where a car gets its power and you say, "well, when I put my foot on the gas, the car moves."  Of course, most cars move because of tiny explosions inside of the engine which push pistons and generate motion energy which the car ultimately transfers through the transmission to the drivetrain and finally the tires.  And it's much more complicated than that in reality if you get into the physics and engineering of it.  A system is no different.

Thanks for your method.

In order to maintain the accuracy of your method which works best as designed for H1 (60 min.) and use the BGX line generating program that authomaticaly install the cross levels ,the filters levels etc.I and the features of many others systems operating only on M30,I had to convert your set-up data as follow.

EMA 28 doubled to 56

EMA 18 to 36

LWMA 8 to 16

LWMA 5 to 10

RSI 14 to 28

I also added  EMA 100

Now everything workes like a charm using only one chart (M30).

Maybe this will help others who like to combine many systems/methods unto one screen.

The main objective was to duplicate the positions of the moving averages from H1 to M30.This way the intersection points levels are now on H1 to the same levels on M30.

I have implemented many forex strategies and found that many use M30 as their favourite period .I also downloaded templates to install on Metatrader4

but a lot of them do not work when you toggle from a higher time frame down to M30.I still have a favorite set-up grouping SiDuS D1/H4/H1/M30/M15/M5 and even M1 to analyse price action.

I swing trade mostly using M30 modified to include bits and pieces from about 8 systems to give me what I need on that one chart.

I then enter pending on-stop orders many times in both directions,always with stop loss and sometimes ..take profit points.If the above is not clear, let me know.

--- 帖子 #108 ---
I don't agree.  It seems to me that the Parabolic SAR is more general and doesn't hit the entry and exit timing nearly as well as using the MA's.  I've looked at the SAR with the settings you suggest and while it does "generally" follow the same trend, I don't think it has nearly the same accuracy.  Now, you might be able to modify the settings to do so - I don't know.  But if you take the 4hr USD/CAD, the SAR overlaps changing trends greatly while the moving averages were far more accurate.

I think another issue with using the SAR is it takes longer for people to get used to an indicator that displays the way it does.  We're simply used to moving averages and the way they more directly appear to relate to the pricing. Not that this is a valid reason to discount it's legitimacy as an indicator mind you..

But, if it works for you, then that's all that really matters in the end.  Each to his own, no?

Hey OrangeRoshan:

You seem to be the one that has implemented SIDUS with the greatest success, so far.  This is my experience:

I'm a great fan of this method.  In my first post I mentioned that I had made 60 pips in two days (with two lots = 120 US$), both on EUR/USD.  But, once I changed to use the method with EUR/GBP I've got MAYOR LOSSES (I've lost the 60 pips and another 100 pips I had made the week before).  Why?

Number 1: This pair is more expensive (spread) - any error will cost twice as much - so this is not a fault of the system (was my problem, as I wasn't aware of the spread cost)

Number 2:

(I can't paste a CHART picture to show you, it seems not to work)

But the two WMA's crossed the tunnel upwards.  The tunnel was opening, and the trade looked good to enter LONG (following the suggestions from the pdf - red tunnel crossed and reopening again).

I entered LONG, it peaked and the two came down like rocks, southwards, crossing the red tunnel in the other direction....i left it there going into -50 pips....SOLD OFF and since the red tunnel AND the WMA's showed that being SHORT was the right thing to do, I did that....one hour later they went back up again, crossing the tunnel for a LONG signal - I've had to go out and loose another 50 pips.....this time I didn't have the nerve to go LONG again......

Since then I've been following the system on the charts, but have not traded with it.....I did not have the courage to follow it again.....If I had, I saw that I could have done some decent pips with EUR/USD.....

I'm looking forward to all of your comments and the continuation of this thread.  We should come up with some refinement of details, like:

- For how many pips MAX is this system good?

- How long should I wait for the red tunnel to open itself? (if you wait too long you're on the last end of the trend and will morelikely catch only the last few pips - incurring the risk of loss).  If you do it too early you can get burnt...

Peter.

I'm afraid Peter this is something you'll have to get used to in Forex. The system hasn't been invented that always puts you on the right side of the trade. The most you can hope for, long-term, is more winners than losers.

It's impossible to ask what's the max pips for a system, it all depands on the currency pair, the timing of your entry, and outside influences.

I would suggest that you go and look at the FF Calendar and see if you placed your trade around the time of a US or EU announcement.

I suspect that's the likely cause of the fluctuation.

--- 帖子 #144 ---
Another thought on your trouble with GBP/USD.  You mentioned waiting for the tunnel to open itself.  All you should be looking for is the tunnel to cross.  Sidus has even said that if the 2 WMA's cross, and the red tunnel is converging like they will cross, he will get in.

If you are waiting for the red tunnel to open up again on the other side you probably are just getting in too late.

--- 帖子 #145 ---
Yes!, it is possible OrangeRoshan. The small detail is that Im not a programmer.

Actually I have ideas for entries, profit taking and stop loss(actually its more a trail stop rather than a stop loss)that can work for an EA.

For entry:

The EA open a trade when both the 5LWMA and 8LWMA crosses both 18EMA and 33EMA. The entry most be accompanied with 3-5 trading positions(depends on the volatility and trendy of the currency pair)

Profit taking:

The TP are based on Fib levels (34, 55, 89, 144, 233). For example if you buy GBP 1.8500, then your TPs are 1.8534, 1.8555, 18589, 1.8644, 1.8733 etc. Again this also depends on the characteristics of the currency pair.

Stop Loss or Trail Stop

The Stop Loss or Trail Stops is activated when the price reach the actual lower EMA in the case that you are buying or when the price reach the actual upper  EMA when you are selling the pair. In a trend there arent  losses actually, because the  actual  EMAs are higher(buy) or lower(sell) than your entry point.

OR when both LWMAs crosses both EMAs

This accompanied with optional Ranging Market Filter plus Time filters can make a promising EA. The CHFUSD and GBPUSD are more suitable for this EA.

Hope everybody can understand what I mean. Any questions or suggestions are welcomed

--- 帖子 #147 ---
GBP/USD with Sidus system actually talk to me. It is very volatile. The bar (closing) will move up & down erotically. With no fundamental's announcement, you can basically figure, where the price will go. Buy/Sell every 10-20 pips.

Eg:

The trend is bullish and very strong. The pin slide downwards penetrating either the support or Fibs. It cant go any lower after diving to more than 20pips (Remember: This is only 1hr chart). Since it cant go sideways, it will only go the opposite direction, which is UP. So, BUY!!

Until it reaches the targeted PIPs, Sell it (100% or 70% & keep the 30%, just in case it goes all the way & break resistence). Then wait until it drops down again, Repeat the process!! Its not scalping, its called knowing your pair, its behaviour & the trend.

When the System doesnt talk to you, DONT TRY THIS ATHOME, ITS VEEEERY DANGEROOOOUS!!

Thanks

--- 帖子 #148 ---
How to talk to your chosen currency pair with your trading system?

Step (1).

Look 1-2 weeks back on the charts. Study the behaviour of the pair.

Step (2).

Look @the indicator. How far were the BUY/SELL signals with the actual price. Get a piece of paper and cover half of your screen (to stimulate the future). Study the signal & imagine an entry. Use TEXT and Labels on the charts to pinpoint your move. Then move the charts slowly and see what happens to your prediction. Pipping or not Pipping, Learn from it!

Step (3).

Look @the gap between the tunnels. Look at your other indicators. Take a peek @ the 30mins charts to draw your support & resistance. Look @the time, and see how it behaves. Look @the bar, read them.... and so on.

Step (4).

When you think you know your pair, Talk to it with confidence. TRADE!! Your instinct (within the boundary of the system) will tell you what to do.

Step (5).

Just a glimpse, the pair will talk to you, telling you what to do.

Exercise it, one pip at a time!

This teaching is Brought to you by a Newbie!

Happy Trading

p/s Thanks Sidus

Actually I have ideas for entries, profit taking and stop loss(actually its more a trail stop rather than a stop loss)that can work for an EA.

For entry:

The EA open a trade when both the 5LWMA and 8LWMA crosses both 18EMA and 33EMA. The entry most be accompanied with 3-5 trading positions(depends on the volatility and trendy of the currency pair) Dunno about 33, but I use 28. When The REDs narrowed inside 5&8, the black hole is formed!

Profit taking:

The TP are based on Fib levels (34, 55, 89, 144, 233). For example if you buy GBP 1.8500, then your TPs are 1.8534, 1.8555, 18589, 1.8644, 1.8733 etc. Again this also depends on the characteristics of the currency pair. Thanks to Vegas

The Stop Loss or Trail Stops is activated when the price reach the actual lower EMA in the case that you are buying or when the price reach the actual upper EMA when you are selling the pair. In a trend there arent losses actually, because the actual EMAs are higher(buy) or lower(sell) than your entry point.

Hi All....

I have a huge contribution to make to this method! I could keep this a secret to myself, but I believe in "You get back what you put out"... So I will put this out to all of you...

I have 2 things to add to this system that I have been trading with huge success...  1st... Instead of 5 & 8 EMA's (too much chop), Use 5 & 12 EMA's. They are way more accurate. I signed up for Pro-Signal in the past and I figured out that all their signals were generated from a 5 & 12 EMA cross on the 1 Hr. chart!

People pay thousands a year for this simple advice.... The truth is... It works. And when you add it to the Sidus Tunnel cross you have the closest thing to the Holy Grail!!!!

2nd... Look at RSI. Calibrate it to 21 on the 1 hr. chart. When it climbs above 50 its on the up trend and stay in until it crosses below the 50 and vice versa for the short!

I've been trading this method with huge success... 959 pips in June so far!!!!!!!!!!!!!

It gets you in the new trades and keeps you out of bad ones!

So....  Look for the 5 & 8 EMA cross first... Then wait for the tunnel cross (18 & 28 EMA) and take the trade on the break out...

MONEY IN THE BANK!!!!!!

I hope this helps!

BAGOVINO

--- 帖子 #169 ---
I'm also a newbie (only been trading for about 8 months) but have traded the original Vegas 1 hour and 4 hour models these past few months. With regards to profit taking, what you may want to try is taking your profits using fib numbers (34, 55, 89, 144 etc) calculated from where the lines cross/intersect.

From my experience using the Vegas models (which is similar to this Sidus method) I have been extremely successful with my trades. I tend to also use those numbers as a gauge. For example...your winning trade hits 55 pips, then 89, then makes it to 110. I know that the next fib number is 144 so if the trade doesn't hit the 144 target, I must take my profits off at the 89 fib.

Hope this helps.

--- 帖子 #211 ---
Cable Dollar is a volatile pair. Whipsaw will lash you a couple of time on each bar. But, the trend is known so, it is less to worry about.

Entering & exiting the market is just logic. Example:

In a Bull market:

Level 1:

Wait until the price dropped below the opening price, @least 5 - 10pips, then enter with 35SL. It will give to a good 5-10 pips margin additional to your 35SL, just in case the demon put some unexpected weight on the Pin bar. Other than that, premature exit with a loss will probable not happen, instead you will gain @least 10pips margin derived from the clever entry + the already known bull trend from our indicator.

Level 2:

Do the above but do not exit and let the profit run to the desired pip target and adjusting the SL when you are over 11pips from the entry to 10SL. This way, you are sure a Pipster already. Please take the spread into account!

Level 3:

Modification of level 2, but chop 50% from your original lot (SELL), and let the profit run until the next crossing. Adjust your stop loss as suggested on level 2.

Level 4:

Do level 1,2,3 and when your dealer allows it, Piping the bar with multiple entry (buy/sell) making the whiplash to work FOR you. Now, the rend is your guardian and the whiplash is your friend!

When you want the whiplash to be your enemy, use trailstop. Meaning I dont recommends it, as it cut your profits unnecesarily, ESPECIALLY when you are trading big lots!!

I hope that helps a bit with your question.

Happy trading with Risk management discipline.

Thanks

--- 帖子 #229 ---
I imagine you could trade price bounces off the 18/28 tunnel as long as the 5/12 EMA's do not cross/pass-thru. Enter after the 5 EMA has turned toward the direction of the original trade with at least a 10 pip spread between the 5 EMA and the tunnel to avoid chop. Also avoid entering if 5 & 12 start to do the "DNA spiral" near the tunnel. Give yourself breathing room, but don't wait to long or SL will be too big. Hope that makes sense.

Something else to consider before taking a bounce is how long the current Sidus trade has been going on.  If profit levels of 89, 144 or higher from the tunnel have already been hit, then a bounce entry may not be such a good idea.

Just an idea based on a similar system I have used in the past involving EMA's on a 1/2 hr timeframe...

--- 帖子 #232 ---
MT4 platform let you hedge, meaning you can have multiple SELL/BUY without exiting your previous trade.

Strategy 1

As long as you are +vely piping due to your early entry. Study the whiplash using the shortterm indicator (BLUE&YELLOW) and buy/sell accordingly for a nice 10pips profits. This takes practice & understanding the behavious of your pair. Volatile pair like CableDollar is my favourite. Use 35SL for whiplash protection. e.g: Bearish trend: When the price hit the lowest, way down 30+ pips, Reverse (BUY) for a good 10-15 pips.

Strategy 2

According to the trend, in NOW case, its bearish for cable$. Wait until the price move 15 to 20pips up, then Short (bearish trend)

Strategy 3

Combination of strategy 1&2.

This is what my mentor (20+yrs trading experience) taught me. He call it 100/30pips system.

Strategy 4

When all indicators confirm the trend. The distance between the 2 tunnels are increasing (trend continue) AND the angle of the 4 indicators are following the trend, then Enter according to the trend with confidence.

I hope this will help a bit.

Happy trading & dont forget Risk Management.

Thanks

--- 帖子 #252 ---
Oops. My mistake. I see your entry point and the cross of the 18-28. I think you made a good entry and your SL was reasonable. You lost one, but thats just part of the game. I always use SL's, but I like to monitor my trades often which sometimes negates the SL and I will bail out manually when the 5 & 8 cross and/or start to do a sideways spiral pattern.

This type of trading strategy is actually two trades stacked on each other (someone else mentioned this earlier) and if played right you can use a very small SL.

I like to watch the 5-8 WMA's ( or 5-12 EMA's if you prefer) and enter with 4-6 lots when they cross close (10-15 pips out) to the 18-28 tunnel. This is my short term/small SL trade. If the trade goes thru the tunnel, then I am in it for a longer term. The nice thing is this: If am already in profit from my short term trade, then I put my SL locked in profit of several or more pips just on the other side of the tunnel after the price leaves 20 or so pips in profit. From here on out it is free pippin'.

If my short term trade starts to go against me, then I bail out and make another entry attempt later while either several pips in profit or losing a few pips. I will never allow myself to lose more than 5 pips on my short term trade before the short term trade has crossed thru the tunnel. I am relying on the momentum of the price to carry me to (and hopefully thru) the 18-28 tunnel. If that isn't happening I am out, pronto. I'm willing to give up a few pips on multiple entry attempts because when the trade eventually does go, it usually goes big.

As the price pulls away from the tunnel in my long term trade, I take profit at fib levels (21, 34, 89, 144) while moving my SL deeper into profit as the next fib level is reached. I usually let the last lot(s) run using a 20 pip trailing stop.

What I am doing is a culmination of several strategies that I have studied.  In case you are wondering, I am demoeing Sidus' method using the above guidelines.  I like it so far  !

--- 帖子 #255 ---
I prefer the 1/2 hr timeframe and my fib levels start where the 8WMA crosses the tunnel. I use fib levels 21, 34, 55, 89, 144 and sometimes 15 if the trade has lost momentum after passing thru the tunnel. It helps to have a basic understanding of the way each pair moves and retraces also. Sometimes you have to take a lot or two of profit early at your discretion if the lower fib levels have already been breached when the 8 crosses the tunnel (i.e. you are at the 55 fib level when the tunnel is crossed by the 8 WMA).

I'm considering moving to the 5 & 13 EMA's to try out. 13 instead of 12 because it is a fibo #  .

Also, I try not to enter a trade in the first 5 minutes or last 5 minutes of a 30 min candle (a habit I got into when I was using Bunnygirl's BGX system) as people may be taking profit at those times and skewing the entry point so that I am in a losing position within minutes of entry.

Most importantly, I'm learning from what I do (I consider myself a mediocre trader at best, LOL).

--- 帖子 #262 ---
Hi Guys,

I just wanted to point out an observation I've made while studying this method over the past couple of weeks....

When the market is trending, there is no doubt that the Sidus method will be very profitable. However, on a week such as this past one where the market was in a range and not really trending one way or another this method is inaffective. You either stay out of the trades because there is no clear signal or you want to trade so bad that you take a trade on a wishy washy weak signal and it turns on you.

In order to trade profitably all the time you need 2 methods... One in a trending market (Sidus), and one in a ranging market.

The method I see that works best for a ranging market is the 5/12 EMA cross with the RSI set at 21 with a 50 level cross!

If you study the charts on the 30 min you will see that either the RSI or the 5/12 cross will precursor the upcoming move, meaning: The 5/12 cross may happen first in which you will wait for confirmation of the RSI cross, or the RSI will cross the 50 and you wait for confirmation of the 5/12 ema cross. Either way it is good for atleast 20 to 30 pips. You also want to use pivots, fibs and trendlines. You can then use it in combonation with the Sidus method. So you take the 30 min trade and it starts to take off. You then look at the 1Hr Sidus chart and if it gives a signal guess what? You just got in super early for a huge profit! If not you continue to take your 20 - 30 pips in the ranging market.

So set up the charts, do some research and tell me what you think...

LOOKS GOOD TO ME!

Bagovino

--- 帖子 #284 ---
Yardie,

Sorry for the late reply, but to make an EA you need to open your MetaEditor (MetaQuotes Language Editor under Tools):

1.  click New

2.  make sure Expert Advisor is checked

3.  click Next

4.  Enter the name of the EA

5.  Click Finish

6.  Then cut and paste your code into the new EA and save

7.  Shut down MT4, restart it and it should appear in your EA list.

Cheers,

Jeff

--- 帖子 #296 ---
If we look at the EUR/USD today on the 5/12/RSI cross system we see the first hint of a sell when the 5/12 cross at 18:00 (which is the time on my platform, yours may vary) Roughly 10:30 am NY time. Then at 20:00 the RSI went under 50. We would take a short position at around 1.2721 (which I did). As of this writing it's 22:00 and price is at 1.2686. Thats 35 pips profit.

This is 35 pips profit while we are waiting for the 1hr Sidus to give a signal. Profit that we would have given up. Now we can either take the 35 pips or hold the position and see if we get the 18/28 cross on the 1 hour Sidus method in which we can add more lots to our position and follow the Sidus method for the rest of the trade. I would also now look to the Vegas 1hr Tunnel System to either take the profit when price meets the tunnel, or wait an see if price crosses the tunnel in which we would hold the trade and follow his system for the rest of the trade.

It seems like these 3 systems link together perfectly. We follow the 5/12/RSI 30 min. first to the 1 hr Sidus. If the Sidus gives a signal we then follow that systen, if not we exit and wait for a new signal on the 30 min system again. If Sidus continues the trade we drop the 30 min. and trade the Sidus. Now when the Sidus and the 1hr Vegas system meet up we either exit if it doesn't then produce a cross on the 1 hr Vegas or continue with the trade, drop the 1 hr Sidus and follow the 1 Hr Vegas for the duration of the trade.

It's a 3 Phase Trading System!

I think this is the best system I have ever seen.... What do you guys think?

Bagovino

--- 帖子 #317 ---
The hourly 18 & 28 EMA's values can be transferred to your 1/2 hr charts by doubling them... Thus the 36 & 56 EMA's. That way you only have to have one chart setup for viewing (the 1/2 hr). You can take the Vegas hrly tunnel and put it on your 1/2 hr chart the same way. Best of both worlds, baby. Try it and see for yourself. The reason your entries are better on the 1/2 hr chart is because you took the 5 & 12 EMA's from the hrly and turned them into hrly 2.5 & 6 EMA's on your hf hr chart by keeping the values the same. The larger the EMA value, the greater the price lag....  Try using the 2.5 (or round it to 3) and the 6 on your hourly chart and you then have the exact entry point as you presently have on the half-hour chart.  Pretty neat, huh?

EMA's are based on the # of periods (in this case candles).

1 hrly candle = 2 half-hr candles. So a multiplcation factor of 2 is used for the conversion from hrly to half-hr.

Hell, you can work this system on 5-min charts if you want.

Can't believe some of you veterans have never used this trick.

--- 帖子 #318 ---
When on the H1 chart, you are taking the average of the last 18 one hour candle to form the line.If you want to use the M30 chart then it would take 36 of the 30 minutes candles to trace the average line in the same location as on the H1.Same goes for the 28.

jlm

Oops! I accidentally uploaded the EA before saving it...the one I uploaded before will not work properly, sorry! I was in a rush to get out the door with the family and goofed. The version attached now is what should have been there this morning.

Now, as for the multiple-take-profit levels: I think the easiest way is to just recode the EA to place several partial orders with individual TPs. In other words, the parameters could say something like:

TPLevel1=15;

TPLevel1Lots=3.0;

TPLevel2=20;

TPLevel2Lots=1.0

TPLevel3=35;

TPLevel3Lots=0.5;

The above would basically be a 4.5 lot order from the entry, which would close 3 lots at +15pips, 1 lot at +20, and .5 lots at +35 pips. Something along those lines. This way, the user could define individual TP levels and sizes. Does this sound good to you guys?  Also, I could write it so that the SL is moved up to the last used TP level; in other words, if we got our first 15 pips, the SL on the other orders would change to +15, so we at least get TPLevel1 worth profit on all lots.  Sound like  a good idea?

On a separate note, do we really want to use TP/SL/TS as the exit? Or would you guys prefer something based internally on the system's signals, for example, if the order is a buy and the RSI drops below 50 OR the 5EMA recrosses the 12, then exit? What do you think?

Please give me any suggestions as to what you'd like, I'll code anything that you guys want (so long as I can do it hehehe...).

Good luck with trading to all,

Gavner

--- 帖子 #348 ---
We probably wouldn't want to have it exit if it recrosses, necessarily...  Because this is really just a preemptive entry for the longer term sidus method based on the 30 minute chart.  So  if it was possible though you could do the following for a short trade:

If 5 & 8 WMA on the 1 hour chart are above the 18 & 28 EMAs, and if the 5 EMA recrosses the 12 EMA to the upside on the 30 minute chart, then exit.  Does that make sense?  Then the opposite for a long trade.

On the exit limit orders, it should be Fib levels calculated from the price at the cross of the 5 & 12 EMAs on the 30 min chart.  The levels that I ahve found to be the best is:  exit 1/3 at 21.  exit 1/3 at 34.  And exit 1/3 at 89.

And on moving the stops up when a limit order get's filled, you wouldn't want to move it to the price it was filled at because you would very likely get stopped out.  probably what would be good is:  the value you were limited out at - 30 pips.

E.G.  Short the USD/JPY at 115.52.  (This was a sell signal here btw)  1st order exits at 115.31.  Limits get's moved to 115.61.  (31+30)  Next order get's exited at 115.18.  Limit get's moved to 115.48.  (18+ 30)  Last order is exited at 114.63.  All of these orders would have been met.  Total pips profit gained = 144.  I did this, or close to it on a trade on the dollar yen earlier.  I posted the charts on those entry signals.  And now here is another example of this on the dollar yen, which I realized that I missed this morning/ last night.

Hope this helps.  If you can understand the above you can also just trade it manually which is what I'm doing.  It's basiclly the sidus method with bagovino's additions/ or organizations.

Hi to all, and my complements to everyone involved in nurturing such a promising strategy - especially to Sidus, and Bagovino who got the ball rolling. this appears to look like a grand slam home run! Bagovino's idea of combining different aspects of this tri-phase process to take into account ranging and trending conditions is simply brilliant!

Since some changes have been made along the way, please take a look to see if my Phase One-Two-Three Rules are correct at this time -

Phase One to Enter Long on 30 minute chart:

RSI (21) goes from < 50 to > 50

5 EMA line goes from < 12 EMA to > 12 EMA line

36 EMA (tunnel line) < 56 EMA (tunnel line)

both 5 EMA and 12 EMA lines < both Tunnel lines (36 EMA and 56 EMA)

are the 5 WMA and 8 WMA now dropped from consideration

at this phase?

Phase Two (Sidus) to Continue Long on 60 minute chart:

once 18 EMA tunnel line crosses above 28 EMA tunnel line

2.5 EMA line continues to be > 6 EMA line

RSI (21) continues to stay > 50

both 2.5 EMA and 6 EMA lines move above and stay above both tunnel

lines (18 EMA and 28 EMA)

Phase Three (Vegas) to Continue Long on 60 minute chart:

look for price to cross from below to above Vegas Tunnel

if it does - then look for exits as per Fib levels outlined by Vegas

Any and all help in sincerely appreciated

traderdp

--- 帖子 #372 ---
So here's the deal guys: It was taking a while to make the EA because there are several different methods out there, and I was repeatedly getting confused about which method people want the EA to use. So, right now I'm trying to write it in a pretty customizable way, so you can choose whether you want 5/8LWMAs or 5/12EMAs or X/Y Simple/Exponential/Smoothed/LinearWeighted for your triggers. The problem is not coding at this point though, but rather the method. Here's a short list, hopefully you guys can help clarify so we can get this thing done soon (more pips for all  ):

1) Using the RSI filter: I think filters are a good idea for any autotrading system, due to the high number of false signals that eat up profit. But here's the thing: RSI doesn't always cross 50 at the same time the triggerlines do(triggerline=general term for 5/12EMA or 5/8LWMA or whatever you prefer). Do we need both signals to enter? Do we need both to exit? I recommend requiring only the triggerline cross for entry (since the RSI usually follows within 1~2 bars) but waiting for RSI and triggerline signals to exit.

2) The Tunnels: Do we look for the triggerlines to cross through the tunnel for entry? Or just to stay in? Or for exit? The Sidus PDF seems to dictate that we use the triggerlines passing through the tunnel lines as entry, and the tunnel lines recrossing counter to our trade for exit. (This will lead to overlaps/hedging by the way, since the fast emas will cross through the tunnel before the tunnel crosses itself in the same direction, i.e. the fast EMA long signal occurs before what would be the previous-short-trade-exit-signal {tunnel line crossing}). However, I think Bagovino's faster-entry-strategy calls for entering on the fast MAs crossing each other... What is the actual exact strategy?? Also what is the Vegas tunnel that traderdp mentioned? Is that part of the strategy?

Sorry I'm confused guys, but I can't really program this without knowing which ways we're doing things. If someone could succintly state an exact set of entry & exit rules, I'd really appreciate it. I can incorporate partial profit taking at different levels, etc... but I need to know the exact strategy.

Thanks in advance and sorry for the delay,

Gavner

Hi Bagovino,

--- 帖子 #416 ---
The 100/30 system is briefly mentioned in the TIGA ABDUL PDF as a TP. It is an alternative to chopping lots sizes, exiting a portion at a time on certain price level or fibs.

The 100/30 is a method to harvest 100 pips within a single 30 pip OHLC. eg. Bullish Trend. Prices goes until your TP 10pips, then you exit. Prices then drop -5pips. Which is below your 1st exit position in a bullish trend. Enter position and take TP 10 pips again. It then dropped -15pips, enter buy again, as you know the trend is bullish. Exit again at your first exit point.

The purpose is to bank-in pips and continue the entry like you never exited. THe 9SMA makes it easier to do, as you know the 12EMA still havent cross the 5EMA. This means the trend is still in effect and piping the bar is more convenient.

I hope that helps a bit.

Sometimes you need to give the trade some time to materialize. Because the EMA and RSI cross and then go back slightly 5 minutes after doesnt mean that the trade has gone bad. This is why stop loss is important. I think 20 pips is a good stop loss on the 30 minute chart -- maybe 25 pips. Another thing you could do is just close out the trade if the RSI hit 45 or less on a LONG position or 55 or more on a SHORT position.

--- 帖子 #494 ---
I used to use the VT platform. THis system is easy to set up on it.

Just click on add indicator 4 times, once for each MA.

First time select 18 for period and Expo. under type

2nd time select 28 for pereod and Expo. under type

3rd time select 5 for period and either expo or weighted under type

4 time select 12 or 8 for period etc.

change the color of the 5 and 8 to blue and yellow

I made the lines a little thicker also so they are easier to see.

also I added the RSI and set the period to 21

--- 帖子 #519 ---
Here it is,

EMA 5= dotted blue

EMA 12=dotted yellow

EMA 34=pink

EMA 55=pink

RSI 49/51 above 51 buy

below 49 sell

StepRSI settings 14,5,15

BrainTrend2StopLine==The yellow line is a long position SL and the blue line is a short position SL in my charts.

Vegas 1 hr tunnel

There are differant ways a person can add to a position and subtract from a position so I am not going to go into that. I wanted to talk with some people about that and it doesnt seem to happen. So, we won't go into that part. I will just talk about entry, SL and TP.

To enter a long,

1. Look to see if the blue and orange line is above the purple line on the StepRSI

2. Make sure RSI is above 51.

3.Make sure the 5 EMA has passed through the 12 EMA to the upside.

To enter short,

1. Look to see if the blue and orange line is below the purple line on the StepRSI.

2. Look to see if RSI is below 49.

3. Make sure the 5 EMA has passed through the 12 EMA to the down side.

SL is where the braintrend2 indicator comes into play. It will put lines above and below price. When you enter a trade, for short, make it one pip above the brain trend line and for a long, one pip below.

Vegas 1 hr tunnel. This is where you will take profits or even add to a position. This can be used in a couple ways. This is the part of adding and taking away from a position that I would like to work on with others. I have a good idea on how to do it but, like everyone used to tell me when I was younger, 2 heads are better than one.

I am still working on this system to see if there is some other filter to be used for something.

One thing everyone needs to remember, 30 minute charts WILL have more losers than the 1 hr charts.

I hope I haven't left anything out.

--- 帖子 #529 ---
Hi Everyone,

I just wanted to say a few things here....  I've noticed a few members on this thread, probably newbies, complaining of a few losses and asking the same things over and over. And that's ok, I did that also at one time. Thats how we learn. However, you must realize that no system is 100%. You cannot expect it to be as easy as two lines cross here and one crosses here and BAM!!!! You've got 200 pips!

You have to use other elements in conjunction with this or any other method. For instance, I use Pivot points, weekly and daily, Cam lines, Fibs, MACD, multiple time frames, and most importantly... Trendlines. Right now for instance, there is one hell of a strong upward trendline on the EUR/USD. It is generally bullish on higher time frames meaning be carefull whenever you short it right now until it breaks the trendline. If it were bearish on the higher time frames you'd want to take only short positions, and longs only for a short time on a retracement, and thats risky.

So please for your own accounts sake follow the system that works best for you. 2 people can follow the same exact system yet one will make money and one will lose. So if this one doesn't work for you there are hundreds or thousands out there that will!

Whichever system you chose to base your trading on, use these other factors and your own good judgement with sound money management and you will succeed as a trader!

I hope this helps some of the new guys!!

A bit of tough love from...

Bagovino

--- 帖子 #539 ---
Before anyone goes and starts to trade with the indicators I put on there, make sure you know what you are doing and not find this thread and just start trading this way. Adding to a system makes one think things should get better. Many times, it will make things worse. The simpler the better. People are always looking to improve things they find to make it work out better for themselves. Here is an example of what I mean... How many people do you know that have bought a car be it new or used. They run that sucker so long it dies. It got 35 or 40 miles to a gallon and ran for 200,000 miles. They go to buy their next car and that thing get half the gas mileage and lasts only half as long. They say " why can't they make it like they used to?" That car company that made the car knew how good it was but guess what, yup they wanted to improve it and make it "better" and differant. Now, that example may have went a bit too far but, if you take the original system introduced in this thread, nothing may needed to be added and it will work better than anything you will find.

I did kind of go indicator crazy there for a while and wonder what is the best thing to do. I have chatted with a few people in the last couple days and am pretty much back at a few MAs and RSI. I am glad though that I did put all that stuff out there for you guys to mess with to see what you could come up with though. So, on to my next project.  Posting a rundown of a few MAs and the RSI.    If there are a few changes I miss, please inform so the newer readers know what is going on.  And like I said before, there is a guy I know that would like to get a website up based on this also.

--- 帖子 #540 ---
30 minute chart

5 and 12 EMA

RSI(21) 50

Short= 5 crosses 12 from top to bottom, RSI crosses from above 50 to below 50.

Long = 5 crosses 12 from bottom to top, RSI crosses from below 50 to above 50.

We then switch to the Sidus system.  See if price goes through the 18/28 tunnel.  If it gets through the tunnel and the 18 and 28 MAs cross, we then look at the Vegas Tunnel to take profits.

HM, is that it? I know there are people out here that want it all in one post and it seems like it isn't happening.

--- 帖子 #543 ---
That's pretty much the guts of it.

I just wanted to add that I have been running with this on demo for about a week. All was going well until y'day when both trades I was in got stopped...and by a huge move too. Reason? I wasn't paying attention to upcoming news announcements.

As simple as it is, this system appears to work.  But, you gotta pay attention to what is happening. If there's upcoming news, weigh up your options. Never let a winning trade become a losing trade.

There's no "failure" or "shame" in standing aside if you're unsure what reaction news will bring. Print out FF's calendar and staple it to your screen!

Cheers,

Artamon.

--- 帖子 #548 ---
The StepRSI as seen in the chart I posted has a blue, orange, and purple line.  One way to confirm taking a position is to make sure the orange and blue lines are on the same side as the RSI(21) before opening a trade.  You can also put a Level 50 in it just like the regular RSI.  If all three lines are on the correct side of the 50,  I think it shows a stronger trend.   Time will tell how well it could work.  I did edit my post a little to explain the Step RSI better.

Renasdad hit it right on the head! If your trading the 30 min cross look to the 4hr and 1 hr to get the trend and trade only in that direction. This will increase your winning trades 10-fold. It's a very expensive lesson I once learned!!!

Here is what I do.... I use the Vegas 4hr charts only to identify the trend. I do not trade the Vegas 4hr method. If it shows long I wait for the 1 hr to show long. You can even zoom in to the 15 min. to get an idea of when the 30 min may cross because it will show up there first.

--- 帖子 #587 ---
I didn't catch it.  Although, I am attaching a chart to show something.  This chart is what I am talking about with posting charts and a little explination.

5 EMA crossed the 12 EMA with RSI  on the 30 min chart.  Notice how the 5 is bouncing off the 12 but not crossing it.  The RSI however is going from below to above the 50 line.  The 5 EMA is filtering out the RSI to keep us from going long.

The second chart,  1 hr with the 18/28 EMA and Vegas tunnel.  Notice price touched the tunnel and retraced forming a pinbar.   After the  5 and 12 crossed on the 1 hr, and then you opened the trade, it would have only needed a 25 pip SL to keep you safe.

--- 帖子 #591 ---
Congrats to all who have contributed. Have been spending all my time trying to keep up with the posts! There seems to be differing opinions with regards to the use of higher timeframe trend evaluation as a "filter" for the 30min. Bagovino mentioned his lessons with regards to only trading in line with the 4h & 1h trends. However the previously mentioned trade with yesterday's EurUsd fall was AGAINST the trend, but was successful. Also, the idea of the trade progressing through 3 phases or stages where phase 1=30min chart (5/12EMA cross with RSI 50 cross) followed by phase 2 = the modified 1h SIDUS (using 5/12 EMA rather than 5/8 WMA's), followed by phase 3 = the Vegas 1h tunnel would seem to suggest that the first entry (the 30 min chart) would often be at the point of a trend reversal (against the trend). This would often agree with Vegas' point that once the price reaches one of the outer fib channels, its screaming exhaustion. You'd then get a reversal, a phase 1 entry (against the trend), then if the reversal is successful, a phase 2 confirmation then possibly phase 3 with a cross of the vegas 1h tunnel. Wouldn't it be frequently after phase 3 that you'd finally get agreement with the trend? How does the idea of ignoring the prevailing trend IF price is beyond one of the outer 1h Vegas fib levels (screaming exhaustion) sound?

<HR style="COLOR: #d1d1e1" SIZE=1><!-- / icon and title --><!-- message -->do you mean that you only stay in a trade one or two bars looking for a 10 pip profit and then exit when you hit your goal?

Yes & No

In my PDF i mentioned about using the 30mins most of the time. This is primirily used for 100/30 system. But actual trading decisions are based on the 1hr

1. 10pips is the ultimate goal. Its easier to get & duplicate. Sometimes when you target more than 10pips, it ended up becoming a losing trade. ROB Booker recommends it as well (www.robbooker.com).

10pips x 1 lot = $1
10pips x 10 lots = $10
10pips x 100 lots = $100

same 10pips with different monetary value.

Regarding exiting, at my level (trust me, you dont want to know) i trade more than 1 lot. I do 3 things:

1. Exit at 10pips with 50% of my lot
2. Stay on the trade with remaining 50% when:
a) 12EMA is very near or touch or approaching the 5EMA (most of you guys are just thinking about to trade, while Im already half way, already banking in the pips). The reason I know the next reentry signal is about to begin. So its safe to ride.

b) Support & Ressistance lines dictates the right trend

c) The Fibs are very far at least 20pips minimum

d) My elliot waves predict a trend advantages to me.

3. Exit 20% everytime it hits additional 10pips

4. The last lot will stay. Exit only when 9SMA cross the 5EMA
And then are you looking for a reentry ?

When 12EMA cross the 5EMA

"Enter position and take TP 10 pips again. It then dropped -15 pips, enter buy again, as you know the trend is bullish"

At the early stage of entry, 10pips is already being made. But price can dance around the bar like a bunjee jumping. After you exit with 10pips, wait until it retrace, then enter and start all over again. This however only possible when your platform allows multiple entry without adjusting your remaining lots. MT4 allows it.

do you only buy again if the price dropped, and if so by how much before entering again with a buy?

The half number of lots your previously exited. Targeting only 5pips. Because it is quiet risky.

And when you later said in the same post, " Exit again at your first exit point"

Retracing with reverse. Not recommended when you dont have enough practice.

--- 帖子 #655 ---
OK:

For the ones interested in the Russian indicator. Here is the story and what I have so far.

I searched for a day or two everything about LEADING indicators.

Then I found a thread on another forum (i have to search which one it was) where some traders where discussing this kind of problem.  One of the posts explained about this Russian indicator that works "wonders"  .  I've downloaded the indicator and have been playing around since then.

They have problems, like LAGGING indicators have theirs.  The main problem is that they sometimes MIS-LEAD you!  It is interesting to see that this indicator draws a blue line BEFOREHAND and I have seen the bars follow it pretty close ON SOME DAYS....on others (SPECIALLY NEWS!) this thing sucks.  But I guess every mathematical tool gets puzzled with NEWS.

I have attached this indicator into the following charts/currencies:

EUR/USD -- on the 30 MIN chart with Bagovino settings, on the 1H chart with SIDUS original settings and on a 4H chart with KNIFE settings (this is for users of the privat section of this Forum - James16Group)

It worked best, so far on the 30 Min chart with the following settings: 36 hours, 8 m and iO=5.  These aren't the original settings.  I have tested several combinations, all on the same chart and these where the best in combination with the 30 Min chart.

To see if the "predictions" work, I took screenshots with the projections on it and have taken screenshots all along the way of the projected line, to have a visual confirmation of the path of the bars.  I have not traded accordingly, but I could have made some extra pips - even trading COUNTERTREND (which is good for the TIGA ABDUL method that OrangeRoshan uses).

EUR/GBP -- only on 30 Min charts with Bagovino settings (after seeing that it works well on the EUR/USD counterpart i guessed it would sit well on this chart as well).  I haven't collected too much information here, as I have with EUR/USD.  So, still working.

USD/JPY -- same as EUR/USD - used it on 4H Knife, 1H SIDUS and 30M Bagovino - BUT results are somewhat prone to errors - I honestly don't know why.

HERE IT IS - READY FOR RELEASE.  Let me know what you think.  I hope it makes you money.  On your own risk.  I have not modified anything, just the settings once it is attached to the charts.

Maybe some Math wiz can figure out what it does exactly.

Wish you pips.

--- 帖子 #678 ---
You just need to add an SMA to your chart?

If I'm not mistaken, that's easy (at least with my platform).

Go to Insert/Indicators/Trend/Moving Average and open the Parameter tab.

Set Period to 9, MA method to Simple and click OK. That's all it takes...

--- 帖子 #702 ---
I traded it: got ready in advance and then when the data came in I followed up the whole 1 min bar. That was easy beautiful and simple! But that's not what I want to talk about.

Regarding RSI. It is not enough to know that RSI is above 50. And this is a real problem. We want to credit the MAs cross only when RSI of the bar before the previous bar was less than 50, then when the previous bar was closed, we want to know that is above 50, and only then we want to trade the cross. In other words, we wanna have a numeric RSI value from the previous bar and the current bar and compare them. I am not a MQL4 programmer, (programmer, though), this is a new language to me, but trying to make EA for Sidus method, I bumped into this problem and while not having enough experience with MQL4 (and having a full time job), until now I didn't solve the problem. But at least, I know where the problem is! Otherwise you don't want to jump into a trade when the price has exhausted itself and RSI is above 70 or somewhere in the middle between 50 and 80.

If that could be done, all of us will be just fine.

Regards,

lietuve

Hi Hafiz,

Copy the EA into the expert folder of your MT4. When done, exit the MT4 program, then restart. Click navigator in the top right of your platform. Look for expert, then click the EA. Activate it by clicking the Expert advisor's button mid top of your platform.

Happy Trading!!

Thanks for sharing CT. May I ask, what is the function and usage of 144/169 EMA's? How to use them

cheers.

--- 帖子 #719 ---
It's all about momentum over the short to medium term. Lower ema's produce momentum signals that give trading signals that are to short-term to trade profitably. In other words, the dreaded whip-saw. It may go in your direction for 3 minutes and 6 pips, then it rolls over and crushes you. Higher ema's produce momentum signals that are to long-term. In a trending currency market retracements are where you can re-establish profitable positions. They stop very close, if not exactly on the 144 and 169 1 hour ema; the tunnel.

CT

<o> </o>Time to trade, daily average ranges, other:

<o></o><o></o><o> </o>  - One thing I also do is to know the daily average range of each currency pair from high to low and gauge the movement potential for that 24 hour period. This is one important factor that should be considered when trading. For example, the daily average range for the EUR/USD is 120 pips... and within the last 24 hours, it has moved 110 pips, so I expect it to slow down at this point. I captured 108 and jumped out since last post an hour ago.<o></o>

<o> </o>

<o> </o>- The best times to trade are usually at the London Market opening and the US Market openings.<o></o>

<o> </o>

<o> </o>- On average, each currency has an opportunity to move every 1.5 days using the sidus method, old and new.<o></o>

<o> </o>

<o> </o>- I just keep in mind the average daily ranges for each currency pairs which show me the potential high and lows within each 24 hour period.<o></o>

<o> </o>

<o> </o>- In a trending currency market retracements are where you can re-establish profitable positions. They stop very close, if not exactly on the 144 and 169 1 hour ema; the tunnel.<o></o>

<o> </o>

<o> </o>- No fibs and no pivot points (needed).<o></o>

<o> </o>

--- 帖子 #771 ---
Yes, just modify the properties of the indicator.

for 18 and 28 EMA :

FasterMode : 1

FasterMa : 18

SlowerMode : 1

SlowerMa : 28

for 5 and 8 LWMA

FasterMode : 3

FasterMa : 5

SlowerMode : 3

SlowerMa : 28

The parameters for the mode are 0=sma, 1=ema, 2=smma, 3=lwma

I would stay away when there are news releases unless the particular news that's coming out is insignificant in terms of spiking prices.

The Red news in Forex Calender at Forex Factory are definitely the ones most of us would stop trading (other than news trading), and the Orange ones are the ones that may or may not move the price depending on the economic figures that's being released. I would say yellow ones are 99% safe, meaning they would not have immediate and significant effect on the price. (Correct me if I'm wrong on this one)

--- 帖子 #809 ---
Hello guyz, here is a lilttle modification i made to the RSI indicator. It plots RSI as colored Histogram. And below are the conditions:

Long:

If RSI > 50   AND    5ema > 12ema    ==== Bright Green colored bars

if RSI > 50   AND    5ema < 12ema    ====  Light Green colored bars

Short:

if RSI < 50   AND    5ema < 12ema    ==== Bright Red colored bars

if RSI < 50   AND    5ema > 12ema    ==== Light Red colored bars

This is not signals for entry, but it will give you visual indications of rules being met for different condications.

If you feel its usefull then use it, if you feel like its confusing, then ignore it

--- 帖子 #852 ---
That is my main thing I am working on. We have a good entry signal.  That is no problem there.  Now to maximise this, we need a good exit signal and SL.  And with taking profits, it depends on where the signal was produced in relation to the overall trend.  If we are in an uptrend and we get a buy signal on a dip, our TP would be greater than if we get a signal on a little retrace.  That is why I like the Vegas tunnel idea.  We see where the signal is in relation to the tunnel.  If price is just above the tunnel, and we get a buy signal, we have 3 fib lines to take profit at.  If we are at the outter fib level of the tunnel and we get a sell signal, there is a chance we have 6 or 7 take profits we could use.

--- 帖子 #853 ---
Here is an example of the 1 hr Vegas Tunnel.  I know there are other signals I didn't mark.  But, look what price did after those signals.  It stalls at the fibs and the tunnel.    Notice way to the right,  the blue arrow.  That is where I would look for a long signal to go back the other way.  The best setup is where price is at the outter fibs.  But, notice where price has stalled.  I think Vegas tunnel is the best thing when it comes to taking profit.

Hey Guys....

My first post on the Sidus thread.  Thank you all for your very useful comments and thoughts.  I have been playing with this system for the last week on TradeStation (makes it tough to share indicators) and have had great results.

So, here are some of my thoughts.

First, to help with the RSI chop chop during a range situation, take note of RSI difference (current bar to previous bar) on the bar which makes the RSI cross above / below the 50.  I have found that in some channeling situations this difference to be very small; < 3 (speaking in absvalue).  I'm also speaking of the 1H.

Second, for exits.  I am taking a vegas 1H approach.  I like to think of it as "expectation."  Chances are unless there's a very very strong trend the price will retrace when you've hit the 3rd / 4th fib, so when this happens I tighten up my exits.  I'm still toying with different indicators for this, but inorder to keep symmetry I like to use periods of 5, 9, and 12.

--- 帖子 #868 ---
Hello jonesla9,In my short but quite profitable time as a trader , this is what I think people(which is what I'm doing at the moment), need to do with the sidus system(or in fact any system)

First, decide on an exact rule for entry.Then, look at historical charts, and applying your entry rule, decide on what looks like a reasonable stop.Then, you need to decide how your going to follow the trade, if it moves in your direction.Then, you need to look at % efficiency for hitting(these are only examples, you decide) 20, 40,60, 80, 100 pips profit.Now, we are trying to make money within certain time frames.For example it's no good having a system that is down for the first hundred years but makes you a million in the second hundred. that might be ok if you have kids but no good for you, you'll be dead.so, your system needs to give an acceptable number of pips(YOU decide what's acceptable) to this little sum- pips per trade multiplied by trades per(shall we say month?)month.If you're day trading using say hourly charts I would say a couple of months backtesting and at LEAST 2 or three months demoing is enough to get your stats.It's not over yet.If you decide to go live you need to continually monitor your statistics, adding each trade you take to them(or any trade you miss which fits into your rules), making sure that the stats still tell you that the system is still profitable.If a system is profitable for the first three months of 2006 it might not be for the next three months.You need to continually monitor it and decide if you think it is still profitable.

Does this help?

If I've missed anything(not money management please) please tell me, or if anything dosn't make sense please ask . I've been drinking southern comfort.

How you manage your own money is up to you.

I haven't tested this system yet. I just want to say that it's perfectly possible to backtest a crossout system. the problem you mentioned above, that a signal quickly reverses itself after it's occured, can be safely resolved by taking the signal only at the end of a bar, e.g. before a bar completes, don't take the signal. this may give you less profits, but it'll save your account by filtering out a lot of non-crossouts. good trading.

--- 帖子 #886 ---
renasdad, stricko108,

Whenever I see insignificant crosses like that I like to look at the slope value of the line.  I take the slope of the 5EMA with a period of 12 and the slope of the 12EMA with a period of 5.  Looking at both of these slopes together will show you if the cross is significant enought to constitute a "real" cross.  Additionally, I look at the change of the 5EMA which caused it to cross the 12EMA.  I know these things are fundamental, but when you're automating the system 100% it's very important for the computer to know that.  Computers are dumb machines which can only do what you tell them to.  Unfortunatly I'm using TS so I can't code these things into the metatrader EA you guys have been working on.  I'll make the switch soon enough though.

I haven't looked at the ATR yet.  I'll check into that.  As for < 'some number' what I think you should do is normalize the ATR value.  When you normalize the value of an indicator it compares the current indicator value to the value over some period.  This gives you a value from 0 to 1, or 0 to 100.  This allows you to compare the indicator to itself, and get a better view of where it "came from."  I find this to be most useful as long as you're sample periods don't get to long.

Thoughts?

mrLogik

--- 帖子 #892 ---
Matt...  I dont use metatrader but I can explain how I do it in TS.

Here's the sydo code.

//

inputs: xInd(current value of indicator), p(period / number of samples);

1. get xInd

2. Find the lowest value of xInd over a period P.

3. Find the highest value of xInd over a period P.

4. Calculate the range (3. - 2.).

5. return (1. - 2.) / 4.

The returned value is the normalized value

//

I hope this helps.  Also, as I keep saying slope over and over again I realize that some people think of slope as direction of a trend line.  At least this is what vegas says is slope in his 4H paper.  The way I mean slope is mathametically.  Slope = rise / run.  This is good (conservative) for exits because you get to see when the EMA you're using for an exit is slowing down rather than turning.  In this instance you are getting out while the move is still going in the direction of the trade, but you better predict when the EMA is going to turn, rather than waiting for it to turn....

Happy Coding.  Let me know if you don't understand anything.  I'll be awake for the next 4 hours or so.

mrLogik

--- 帖子 #937 ---
One thing I have heard over and over again.  Backtesting doesn't give very good (true) results.  As for filtering the false signals, the false signals are usually made when price is ranging so, the only way to filter out that is to find an indicator that will indicate when price is rangebound.  All indicators are lagging so, that is very hard to do.  So,  the best filter here for me is my eyes.  I'd have to say sup/res or something like that.  Yes ATR will show when price is trending and when it is range bound.  But, with ATR, wouldn't we get 2 or 3 false signals before ATR indicates price is ranging?  I am done looking for indicators that will make this better.  Simple is great.  a couple crosses with a bit of price action sometimes.  No matter what system a person uses or who uses the system, there will always be losses.  The key is to get the system to give small losses (SL) with large gains (TP/Exit).  I know that is the key so, since we have an awesome system we are working on,  Why not focus our attention on where the SL and TP/Exit should be?

--- 帖子 #941 ---
reanasdad.

I have heard that idea bandied about before. Whatever time frame you are trading wait for the close of the next bar before entering a trade.

Trouble is, if you are trading the 4hr or dailies then you are entering at just about that time the winners are getting out, so if you were planning to go long, the earlier longs would be passing the batten to you at just about the high of the present move.

Better still look at the longer time frames without any indicators. Observe price action. Recognise support & resistance. Take note of recent Fib retracements.

Support or Resistance is an area not a set number value !

--- 帖子 #946 ---
Ren,

I am using the RSI as my "trigger."  I only allow 3 bars max after an RSI cross to enter a trade (waiting for the 5/12 cross).  If you wait to long you may enter at the end of the move.  Although using this method you give up some good moves, the ratio of good moves missed to bad moves taken is about 1:4.

As far as using larger time frames (4H / D) for trend direction, I agree.  Price action is the best way to go when your trading the 30 / 1H for in this method.  Anything else lags to much; you'll never get an entrance.

mrLogik.

I sense the Gold rush has settled here with the ebb/flow of fresh information.

As I said before  it is all a matter of individual perception.  Any combination of indiactors will yield good trading.. So as long as the settings are primed per the time interval you are watching.  Being as the actual control of the forex flow is cross breed between different currencies, this is your true indication of direction.  As we find that the USD/YEN is opposit of the EUR/USD  most all the time with the exception of a stronger tug from say the GBP/USD as that is the buddy currency to the EUR/USD  or say the USD/CHF pulls against the USD/YEN as it is the buddy currency to the USD/YEN notice I call them buddy currencies as they complement each other in same overall direction.  Now lets throw in a curve...  EUR/JPY   This a Part time lover to the USD/YEN sometimes it will compliment the USD/YEN as a buddy and on other occasions it will do it's own thing such as tonight and for some Morning..  8-18-06  it had all time highs over-night while the yen and euro were basically at a total stand still..  KEY::::  watch the key bid offer levels for the currency you like to trade as well as the bid offer levels of the counter currency.  This will explain to you total technical traders why you get whipsaws you can't figure out most of the time but not all as nothing is infinate with this ride called forex.  The Big dogs like to run stops on each other and we sometimes get caught in the wake..  i.e. option expires a favorite chase down.. Perception is key to it all!  You can program a million setups and if you can't see or at least reolize what going on out the runway, you trades will get run-down! A good portion of the time.  You all have been told it's all about support and resistance  I buy You sell  Some hesitate then enter.. This all contributes to what we all know as the trend. Note the attached images as an example of mirrored effects on flow and stall dependant on in the currency or out of the currency influx

Keep it safe

--- 帖子 #988 ---
using Bagovino settings

EMA 5 on close

SMA 9 on close

EMA 12 on close

RSI 21 on close Fixed minimum on 30%,Fixed maximum on 70%

add LWMA 100 on close.

Now go to M5 and observe when the slow MA,s 5-9-12 cross over the 100MA,this gives you a solid signal to exit your short entry and enter a long one.The RSI on M5 also usually crosses over the 50% line at the same time.

Only use the above after or near the ema 5 crossing the SMA 9 on H1.

I also use MACD set on default (12,26,9) on H1 as an additional confirmation of the move.If the histogram is above water (0) and rising ,I stay in long but as soon as the ascending signal line breaks thu the descending histogram bars ,I take that as a change of trend direction and act accordingly.

If you like ,you can use all the above on H4 and D1.As long as the price bounces above the LWMA 100 you hold on to your long position.You may have to have deep pockets full of money to be able to stay in the trade as the price does its fluctuations.

Pippy the phew stikes again.

jlm

LWMA 5 on close

Yardie,

As I mentioned in my earlier post I followed the signals of Sidus3 setup with attention on an EURUSD H1 chart. Yesterday at GMT 10:00 there was a signal to go short (the image of chart attached shows SBFX time, that is GMT +2). The short signal unfolded in three steps:

the EMA(5) bounced back down from EMA(13) at GMT 8:00,

the Stochastic bounced back down from 80 at GMT 9:00,

on Stochastic the %K line fell below the %D line at GMT 10:00, the MACD was below zero and the signal line crossed MACD,

then the price went down approx. 40 pips.

At GMT 11:00 Stochastic's %K line started to rise - first signal to close the order,

at GMT 12:00 Stochastic's %K line crossed up 20 - second signal to close.

At GMT 13:45 the University of Michigan Confidence Survey came out and the market became too choppy for this setup.

A1 Cruiser.

Hardly surprising, all the MA is doing is looking back. In the case of the 62ma it is showing the average price of the previous 62 30minute periods recalculated on the close of the last period.

Price action & S&R levels together with length of candle wicks should be taken into consideration.

to open an indicator in a separate window ...

Change this line ..... (in MT4 MetaEditor) ...
#property indicator_chart_window

<?xml:namespace prefix = o ns = "urn:schemas-microsoft-com:office:office" /><o>to ..........</o>
#property indicator_separate_window

#3. First TP target at fib line - took 1 lot @ 1.2275 (+42)

#4. Second TP target at 4 hr channel bottom @ 1.2250 (ordinarily I'd go to next fib line, but seeing as it's below the trend channel I'll take 1 lot here and the final lot at next fib line @ 1.2240.

--- 帖子 #1007 ---
Ok, basically, we wait for the 5/12 EMA cross and the RSI(21) cross. 5 cross 12 upwards and RSI(21) cross 50 upwards we BUY at the next bar open. Opposite for Short trades.

For me, I take profit at Vegas 1hr Fib levels and tunnel. The indicator is in this thread. Maybe you can incorprrate it.

The only 2 features I would like (at this point in time ) is the ability to enter how many bars are allowable between the 5/12 crossing and the RSI(21) crossing for it to be a valid trade. And, the bar where the 5/12 crosses or RSI crosses to be less than XX (a value I can input) pips in range (H - L).

Edit: Umm, I forgot about SL. SL is set to 30 pips or just above the highest H (or L) over the last few bars. After the first TP is taken, SL should be moved to BE or 30 pips. I then keep it at 30pips after each bar closes, but i never move it to give my trade more room if the trade goes against me.

Cheers mate,

Art...

--- 帖子 #1070 ---
http://www.forexfactory.com/forexfor...achmentid=6866

Read the PDF in the first post of this thread. You must add the 18/28 exponential moving average as these are very much an integral part of the Sidus method.

I don't follow or use the bago method. What I do is when the 5 crosses the 12 I take note but do not enter. I then see if the 5 and the 12 are going to cross the 18 and 28. If they do cross up and are above the 100 EMA I go long and vice versa for short. I do bend the rules from time to time though on the 100 EMA.

--- 帖子 #1094 ---
Hi,

I'll take a shot at it.

Suppose you traded one lot (mini, micro, or standard) of the GBPUSD, and made 30 pips.

That would 30 pips total correct? 30*1 lot = 30 (THIS IS NET PIPS)

Now if you traded 5 lots, making a profit of 30 pips (on each lot), you would make a total of 150 pips. That's 30*5 lots = 150. (THIS IS LEVERAGED PIPS)

Net pips are more indicative of the movement of the pair that was captured. Hope this helps.

regards,

forexpips

--- 帖子 #1095 ---
That would be it. Thirty pips is always thirty pips, it's just that some times those thirty pips are worth more than other times (like 3x as much in this scenario).

--- 帖子 #1096 ---
That is exactly hoe we are doing it.   If I opened a trade with 2 lots and the pair went +30 pips, I would say 60 pips.  If the pair went -30 on 2 lots, I would say -60.  This is how we do it cause we would trade differant size amounts sometimes.  If we have 3 TPs on 1 trade, we have one lot for the first TP.  Then we hit out second TP with our second lot.  Then our third lot with our third TP.

Ok,

I can do that one more time.  Anyone reading my journal should know how I am doing it.  I will post here one more time how I am doing it.

It is a little discretionary though, always remember that.  Me and Art chat alot and we help each other to either take a trade or encourage each other to stay out and we both look at each others ideas to see what should be done.  So, the results for others may not be like ours.

1 hr charts only.  5/12 cross, RSI/50 cross, Vegas 1 hr Tunnel.  Risk models change depending on which pair is being traded.

We also use the emacrosswithrsi(3) indicator provided by Peterdxb.  That is only there to show when the price has crossed and the RSI has crossed.  We take trades at the outter fib line of the Vegas Tunnel or we take trades very close to the tunnel.  That is where the discretion comes in.  Anyone can see when the crosses happen.   The hard part is which ones to take.  Take a 4 hr chart and zoom way out as far as possible and see what price has done in the past.  Some times you can make a trade 3-4 hrs before the crosses have happened by the fib lines and the trend.

Questions are welcome.  I'll do my best answering them.

--- 帖子 #1105 ---
I want to explain something about how I placed those lines cause I know there are some out there wondering.  I place the lines according to the fib lines when the trade was open.  I always put the TP -1 or -2 from the fibs to be safe.  Also, if you notice, the fib lines have moved away from where the original TP was at the beginning of the trade.  A person can adjust the TP as the tunnel  cllimbs/falls.  When going against the major trend, the conservative approach would be to move the lines with the fibs.   When going with the trend, the conservative approach would be to leave the lines where they are.

--- 帖子 #1124 ---
Money Ma$ter,

I am active on other forums but read here on a regular basis (This is my first post on FF so I hope I haven't broke any rules)...

I noticed that you said you are using FIB levels for exit. I use Murrey Math levels for taking profit around a tough S/R level and find them very accurate and good for safe entry as well. I will attach three of them and all are for MT4. If you don't use MT4 you can get a free demo download at www.strategybuilderfx.com with no expiration date on it, but there are many sites that allow you to use it for free so do a search if you don't like the above.

1. MMLevels_VG -This one has "wider" S/R lines and works good for longer term trading (Trading off the 4hr charts).

2. 8376-better... -I mainly use this one. It gives good exit/entry points and it will show different S/R lines on the shorter timeframes than the longer timeframes. I like the levels on the 1hr mainly.

3. Murrey Math Lines F -This one is a little easier on the eyes (dotted lines), and you can use this one to back test.

So if you want to back test use only the Murrey Math Lines F as the others won't be good for a back test but work great when trading with them in real time.

FYI- When I am getting ready to enter a position I look to see where the S/R levels are and usually wait for the trend to break past the closest line if price is close and it hasn't already done so. The best is when you get an entry with your chosen system and the price has just broke below/above a S/R level. You will see that this will not only help with exit, but works great for safe entry as well (If using a tight stop this is even more important).

*You can use these when placing stops as well.  I use them and place my stop above/below a MM level by about 6 pips and find it works much better than just placing a random 25-35 pip stop.

Anyway, I hope this will help to improve your profit! I am 90% F/A (news trading) trader as well so I understand where you are coming from. Also, thanks for all your posts on news trading!

Mike

***Once you have MT4 installed here is how you use them...

1. Copy these indicators. Right click on the start menu and go to "Explore"- Then click on the folder called "programs" - Then scroll down to the MT4 program and click on it -Then look for the folder named "experts" and click on it- Then you will see a folder within that one called "indicators"... Paste them in there and then restart MT4 before using.

To apply them to a chart get a chart loaded and then go to the indicators tab and use the "custom" indicators dropdown. Click on the Murrey Math indicator you want to apply. You will not need to change any settings as they are ready to use.

Like I said before I like using them on the 1hr or 4hr chart, but use what works best for you're trading style. I know the above instructions may be common knowledge for you so sorry if that's the case!

***I am not the coder of these and do not take any credit for them. They work very well and were written by someone in a different forum.

Entry Signals! You should only open a position, when the red tunnel is extremly narrow or crossed !

SHORT: 5 WMA & 8 WMA cross the red tunnel downwards.

--- 帖子 #1146 ---
I only got one person that replied to this.  Is anyone doing this?  So many people following this method.  I know there are many differant ways and "tweaks"  people have done.  Is anyone actually keeping track?  If not, that is not a good thing.  I am not posting this for my benefit.  I am doing it for everyones benefit.  You take notes on your trades, SL/TP/Time of open/signal.  Do all that stuff and then once the TP is hit or the SL is hit, you take notes on what made that trade work or didn't work.  If you guys are just taking a trade and it worked, and you have no notes to look at to see why you took that trade, you won't know what worked.  If you take a trade and no notes and that trade doesn't work, you won't know why it didn't work.  Then after the week, you go back over your trades and see what went wrong on certain trades and see if there is a pattern.  If one thing keeps popping up, you drop it.   For those of you who think you don't need to take notes, you are wrong.  I used to think like that too.  And for the people that don't want to cause it is too much work or just don't feel like it, then I don't feel sorry for you when you don't understand why this doesn't ever work right.   Please start taking notes if you want to improve you method of trading.  It will only help you.  Imagine having 6 months worth of notes based on one method of trading.  Or after that first 6 months of taking notes and "tweaking", you have 5 yrs of notes.  That is a gold mine of info.  If you think I am full of BS, that's ok.  I know how you feel, I used to think like that.

--- 帖子 #1172 ---
I don't know about you guys, but I feel that contrary to what SIDUS suggested, this method is not always that good for EUR/USD, since the pair moves very irregularly at times with short cycles.

However, I do feel that with his other pair of choice, the EUR/GBP, his method works wonders, 'cause it has more regular, smooth and longer cycles than the EUR/USD.

When you look at SIDUS' original pdf file on page one and you look at his examples on charts, the difference is obvious. He uses 1 example with the EUR/USD (1st chart) and 3 examples with the EUR/GBP.

You can see the example on the EUR/USD chart that most of the times the entry and exit signals of the 18/28 ema's are very delayed. This happens because the EUR/USD movements do not last long enough.

But when you look at the EUR/GBP examples, the entry and exit signals give you plenty of time to ride the trade with profits, as a result of the pair having longer cycles.

Now, you could say that on the EUR/USD all you need is the 5/12 ema crossing to alert you...but I am sure you had the chance to notice that many times such crossing can be reversed very quicly in the exact opposite direction.

As a result I started to look for pairs that I feel have longer/smoother cycles that could work good better with SIDUS's method, and those are:

AUD/JPY

EUR/AUD

EUR/GBP

GBP/CHF

Let me know what you guys think.

Future
